The 9-0 Pools and Decks
=======================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on January 29, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke












 Opening six booster and constructing the optimal 40-card deck from the material inside is one of the most challenging tasks in *Magic*. We wouldn't claim that the seven 9-0 players here at Grand Prix Prague did build their decks to absolute perfection. But their records do suggest that they must have come quite close.




 Now the question is: do you like a challenge? Then load the following Sealed Pools up on *Magic Online* and try to build your own decks! When you're ready you can find [the actual decks that were piloted to 9-0 finishes here](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gppra17/9-0-decks-2017-01-29). (And yes, you can also find them here if you're just curious ...)











#### Dominik Konieczny's Sealed Deck, 9-0 at GP Prague 2017


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
